**End-of-Working Relationship Questionnaire**

This survey aims to gather your thoughts and experiences regarding the end of our professional collaboration. Your feedback will help us improve future interactions.

1. **What was the primary reason for ending this work arrangement?**

	* Company decision

  ***Very Unsatisified***

	+ Effective communication channels established

       Somewhat challenging        
        Very Challenging**

   **Not at all**   
  ***1***    
     2
      3 
       4        
       5

8. Any additional comments, suggestions for improvement, or feedback about our company's processes related to ending a working relationship?

Smart Working Questionnaire


What is your current work arrangement?

  - Full-time office-based worker (5 days/week)

  - Remote full- timer
  - Freelance/Flexible schedule

  - Rarely/Sometimes

1 = Not Important At All

No regular communication outside of work hours
